# <a name="changelog-for-microsoft-graph"></a><span data-ttu-id="12ae7-101">Microsoft Graph 更改日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="12ae7-101">Changelog for Microsoft Graph</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="12ae7-102">此更改日志涵盖了 Microsoft Graph 变更，包括 v1.0 和 beta 终结点 Microsoft Graph API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="12ae7-102">This changelog covers what's changed in Microsoft Graph, including the v1.0 and beta endpoint Microsoft Graph APIs.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="12ae7-103">有关 Microsoft Graph API 已知问题的详细信息，请参阅[已知问题](known_issues.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="12ae7-103">For details about known issues with Microsoft Graph APIs, see [Known issues](known_issues.md).</span></span>

### <a name="outlook-calendar"></a><span data-ttu-id="12ae7-1697">Outlook 日历</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="12ae7-1697">Outlook calendar</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="12ae7-1698">**更改类型**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="12ae7-1698">**Change type**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="12ae7-1699">**版本**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="12ae7-1699">**Version**</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="12ae7-1700">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="12ae7-1700">**Description**</span></span>                          |
| :-------------- | :------------ | :--------------------------------------- |

| :-------------- | :---------- | :--------------------------------------- |

### <a name="hybrid-deployment-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="12ae7-2860">混合部署支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="12ae7-2860">Hybrid deployment support</span></span>
